This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A – PG 6644 – 05 (2023/12)
PRADESHIYA SABHA WARIYAPOLA
NOTIFICATION  MADE  UNDER  SECTION  24  (1)  OF  PRADESHIYA  SABHA   ACT, No. 15 OF 1987
IT is hereby notiﬁ ed for public information that it has been decided under Decis ion No. 2023/12/15/1710 of the Decision 
Book dated 15th December 2023 that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions have not been taken in a proper court 
before the date speciﬁ ced in the said notiﬁ cation, and all roads thoroughfares which have been conﬁ rmed to be deemed to be 
owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola in accordance with the decree announced by that Court, from among the roads and 
thoroghfares considered to be owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola in the Schedule set out in the Notiﬁ cation published 
in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2341/39 dated 20th   July 2023, by virtue of powers vasted under the Orders in the series of 
''Orders with regard to the Preparation of Plans for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas in  the North 
Western Province and publication of advertisements specifying the name list" by  Hon. Governor in the North Western Province 
which has been published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 dated 30th July 2021 and under the order made under  
Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.

Pൺඋඍ I: Sൾർ. (I) – GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF S RI LANKA  – 20.12.2023
 2A
 It is further notiﬁ  ed that a list of such roads and thoroughfares has been included in the Schedule hereto and every road and 
thoroughfares inclued therein shall be deemed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola under 
Sub -  Section (5) of section 24 of the Pradeshiya Sabha Act. 
 L.M.C.S.N.K. Gൺඅൺൻൺൽൺ඀ൺආൺ,
 Secretary,
 the oﬃ   cer who execute powers duties and functions 
 Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola.
18th December, 2023,
Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola.                                                                         
Decision
 In accordance with the Decision  No. 2023/07/10/667 dated 10th  July 2023, I, L.M.C.S.N.K. Galabadagama, the Secretary 
of the Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola do hereby decide that the roads and thoroughfares among the roads and thoroughfares 
mentioned  in the list set out in the Schedule of the Notiﬁ cation published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2341/39 dated 20th 
July 2023, for which a case has not been ﬁ led in the proper court and are included in the Schedule below should be conﬁ rmed 
as the roads and thoroughfares owned by  the Pradeshiya Sabha Wariyapola, by virtue of powers vested under the "Orders in the 
series of "Orders with regard to the preparation of plans for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas in the 
North Western Province and publication of advertisements specifying the name list " by Hon. Governor in the North Western  
Province which has been published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 dated 30th July 2021, and in terms of the order 
made under Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.
